    <!-- Script pour détecter immédiatement le mode sombre -->
    <script>
        // Détecter le mode sombre avant le chargement de la page
        (function() {
            const darkMode = localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === 'true' ||
                (localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === null &&
                    window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches);

            if (darkMode) {
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
            }
        })();
    </script>

<body
    class="font-sans antialiased bg-white dark:bg-dark-primary text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-100 transition-colors duration-300"
    x-data="{
        darkMode: localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === 'true' || (localStorage.getItem('darkMode') === null && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches),
        toggleDarkMode() {
            this.darkMode = !this.darkMode;
            localStorage.setItem('darkMode', this.darkMode);
            if (this.darkMode) {
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
            } else {
                document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
            }
        },
        initPublic() {
            if (this.darkMode) {
                document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
            } else {
                document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
            }
        }
    }" :class="{ 'dark': darkMode }" x-init="initPublic()">

<!-- Modal de recherche -->
<div id="search-modal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 z-50 hidden">
    <div class="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4">
        <div class="bg-white dark:bg-dark-secondary rounded-lg shadow-xl w-full max-w-2xl mx-4">
            <!-- Header du modal -->
            <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-6 border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-dark-primary">

                    Rechercher sur Sama Bac

                <button id="search-close"
                    class="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 dark:hover:text-gray-300 transition-colors">

                        <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const searchToggle = document.getElementById('search-toggle');
        const searchModal = document.getElementById('search-modal');
        const searchClose = document.getElementById('search-close');
        const searchCancel = document.getElementById('search-cancel');
        const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');
        const searchSuggestions = document.querySelectorAll('.search-suggestion');

        // Ouvrir le modal
        searchToggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
            searchModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            searchInput.focus();
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        });

        // Fermer le modal
        function closeSearchModal() {
            searchModal.classList.add('hidden');
            searchInput.value = '';
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        searchClose.addEventListener('click', closeSearchModal);
        searchCancel.addEventListener('click', closeSearchModal);

        // Fermer avec Escape
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape' && !searchModal.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                closeSearchModal();
            }
        });

        // Fermer en cliquant sur l'arrière-plan
        searchModal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (e.target === searchModal) {
                closeSearchModal();
            }
        });

        // Suggestions de recherche
        searchSuggestions.forEach(suggestion => {
            suggestion.addEventListener('click', function() {
                searchInput.value = this.textContent;
                searchInput.focus();
            });
        });

        // Recherche avec Entrée
        searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                e.preventDefault();
                const form = searchInput.closest('form');
                if (form) {
                    form.submit();
                }
            }
        });

        // Script pour le menu mobile latéral
        const mobileMenuButton = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');
        const mobileSidebar = document.getElementById('mobile-sidebar');
        const mobileSidebarContent = document.getElementById('mobile-sidebar-content');
        const mobileSidebarClose = document.getElementById('mobile-sidebar-close');
        const mobileOverlay = document.getElementById('mobile-overlay');
        const mobileMenuToggles = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-menu-toggle');

        // Ouvrir le menu mobile
        mobileMenuButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
            mobileSidebar.style.display = 'block';
            setTimeout(() => {
                mobileSidebarContent.classList.remove('-translate-x-full');
            }, 10);
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        });

        // Fermer le menu mobile
        function closeMobileSidebar() {
            mobileSidebarContent.classList.add('-translate-x-full');
            setTimeout(() => {
                mobileSidebar.style.display = 'none';
            }, 300);
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }

        mobileSidebarClose.addEventListener('click', closeMobileSidebar);
        mobileOverlay.addEventListener('click', closeMobileSidebar);

        // Fermer avec Escape
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape' && mobileSidebar.style.display === 'block') {
                closeMobileSidebar();
            }
        });

        // Toggle sous-menus mobile
        mobileMenuToggles.forEach(toggle => {
            toggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const submenu = this.nextElementSibling;
                const icon = this.querySelector('svg:last-child');

                submenu.classList.toggle('hidden');
                icon.classList.toggle('rotate-180');
            });
        });
    });
</script>

    <!-- Script JavaScript pour le slider -->
    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const slider = document.getElementById('articlesSlider');
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prevBtn');
            const nextBtn = document.getElementById('nextBtn');
            const dots = document.querySelectorAll('.pagination-dot');

            let currentSlide = 0;

            function getArticlesPerSlide() {
                if (window.innerWidth >= 1024) return 3; // lg: 3 articles
                if (window.innerWidth >= 640) return 2; // sm: 2 articles
                return 1; // mobile: 1 article
            }

            function getTotalSlides() {
                const articlesPerSlide = getArticlesPerSlide();
                return Math.ceil(6 / articlesPerSlide);
            }

            function updateSlider() {
                const articlesPerSlide = getArticlesPerSlide();
                const translateX = -currentSlide * (100 / articlesPerSlide);
                slider.style.transform = `translateX(${translateX}%)`;

                // Mettre à jour les indicateurs
                const totalSlides = getTotalSlides();
                dots.forEach((dot, index) => {
                    if (index < totalSlides) {
                        dot.style.display = 'block';
                        dot.classList.toggle('bg-blue-500', index === currentSlide);
                        dot.classList.toggle('bg-gray-300', index !== currentSlide);
                        dot.classList.toggle('dark:bg-blue-500', index === currentSlide);
                        dot.classList.toggle('dark:bg-gray-600', index !== currentSlide);
                    } else {
                        dot.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            }

            function nextSlide() {
                const totalSlides = getTotalSlides();
                currentSlide = (currentSlide + 1) % totalSlides;
                updateSlider();
            }

            function prevSlide() {
                const totalSlides = getTotalSlides();
                currentSlide = (currentSlide - 1 + totalSlides) % totalSlides;
                updateSlider();
            }

            // Event listeners
            nextBtn.addEventListener('click', nextSlide);
            prevBtn.addEventListener('click', prevSlide);

            // Navigation par indicateurs
            dots.forEach((dot, index) => {
                dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    currentSlide = index;
                    updateSlider();
                });
            });

            // Gestion du redimensionnement de la fenêtre
            window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
                const newTotalSlides = getTotalSlides();
                if (currentSlide >= newTotalSlides) {
                    currentSlide = 0;
                }
                updateSlider();
            });

            // Auto-play (optionnel)
            setInterval(nextSlide, 5000);

            // Initialisation
            updateSlider();
        });
    </script>
    
    <style>
        .scrollbar-hide {
            -ms-overflow-style: none;
            scrollbar-width: none;
        }
        .scrollbar-hide::-webkit-scrollbar {
            display: none;
        }
        .scrollbar-default {
            -ms-overflow-style: auto;
            scrollbar-width: auto;
        }
    </style>
    
    <script>
        // Carrousel des produits populaires
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const container = document.getElementById('homeCarouselContainer');
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('homeCarouselPrev');
            const nextBtn = document.getElementById('homeCarouselNext');
            
            if (!container) return;
            
            let currentIndex = 0;
            const items = container.children;
            const totalItems = items.length;
            
            // Fonction pour vérifier si on est en desktop
            function isDesktop() {
                return window.innerWidth >= 768;
            }
            
            // Calculer le nombre d'éléments visibles selon la taille d'écran
            function getVisibleItems() {
                return isDesktop() ? 5 : 2; // 5 en desktop, 2 en mobile
            }
            
            // Calculer la largeur d'un élément
            function getItemWidth() {
                const visibleItems = getVisibleItems();
                const gap = isDesktop() ? 24 : 16; // gap-6 (24px) en desktop, gap-4 (16px) en mobile
                const containerWidth = container.parentElement.offsetWidth;
                return (containerWidth - (gap * (visibleItems - 1))) / visibleItems;
            }
            
            // Calculer le décalage pour un index donné
            function getOffset(index) {
                if (!isDesktop()) {
                    // Sur mobile, on utilise le scroll natif, pas de transform
                    return 0;
                }
                const visibleItems = getVisibleItems();
                const itemWidth = getItemWidth();
                const gap = 24;
                const maxIndex = Math.max(0, totalItems - visibleItems);
                const clampedIndex = Math.min(index, maxIndex);
                return -(clampedIndex * (itemWidth + gap));
            }
            
            // Mettre à jour la position du carrousel
            function updateCarousel() {
                if (isDesktop()) {
                    const offset = getOffset(currentIndex);
                    container.style.transform = `translateX(${offset}px)`;
                    container.style.overflowX = 'visible';
                } else {
                    // Sur mobile, on scroll vers l'élément
                    if (items[currentIndex]) {
                        items[currentIndex].scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest', inline: 'start' });
                    }
                }
                
                // Mettre à jour les boutons (seulement sur desktop)
                if (prevBtn && nextBtn && isDesktop()) {
                    const visibleItems = getVisibleItems();
                    
                    if (currentIndex === 0) {
                        prevBtn.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
                        prevBtn.classList.remove('hover:bg-gray-100');
                    } else {
                        prevBtn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
                        prevBtn.classList.add('hover:bg-gray-100');
                    }
                    
                    if (currentIndex >= totalItems - visibleItems) {
                        nextBtn.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
                        nextBtn.classList.remove('hover:bg-gray-100');
                    } else {
                        nextBtn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
                        nextBtn.classList.add('hover:bg-gray-100');
                    }
                }
            }
            
            // Navigation précédente (desktop uniquement)
            if (prevBtn) {
                prevBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    if (isDesktop() && currentIndex > 0) {
                        currentIndex--;
                        updateCarousel();
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // Navigation suivante (desktop uniquement)
            if (nextBtn) {
                nextBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    if (isDesktop()) {
                        const visibleItems = getVisibleItems();
                        if (currentIndex < totalItems - visibleItems) {
                            currentIndex++;
                            updateCarousel();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // Détecter le scroll sur mobile pour mettre à jour l'index
            if (!isDesktop()) {
                let scrollTimeout;
                container.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
                    clearTimeout(scrollTimeout);
                    scrollTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                        // Trouver l'élément le plus visible
                        let maxVisible = 0;
                        let maxIndex = 0;
                        
                        for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                            const rect = items[i].getBoundingClientRect();
                            const containerRect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
                            const visible = Math.min(rect.right, containerRect.right) - Math.max(rect.left, containerRect.left);
                            
                            if (visible > maxVisible) {
                                maxVisible = visible;
                                maxIndex = i;
                            }
                        }
                        
                        currentIndex = maxIndex;
                    }, 100);
                });
            }
            
            // Réinitialiser lors du redimensionnement
            let resizeTimeout;
            window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                clearTimeout(resizeTimeout);
                resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                    currentIndex = 0;
                    updateCarousel();
                }, 250);
            });
            
            // Initialisation
            updateCarousel();
        });
    </script>
    </main>

    <!-- Modal Newsletter -->
    <div id="newsletter-modal"
        class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 z-50 hidden flex items-center justify-center p-4">
        <div class="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl max-w-md w-full mx-4 transform transition-all scale-95 opacity-0"
            id="newsletter-modal-content">

                    <!-- Champ caché pour le token reCAPTCHA -->
    <input type="hidden" name="g-recaptcha-response" id="g-recaptcha-response-newsletter" />
    
    <!-- Script reCAPTCHA v3 (une seule fois par page) -->
            
        <script src='https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?render=6LemUeseAAAAADBntkIYpNjjo-yrBAeyR8utrb8Z' async defer></script>
        <script>
            window.executeRecaptcha = function(action = 'submit') {
                return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                    if (typeof grecaptcha === 'undefined') {
                        reject(new Error('reCAPTCHA not loaded'));
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    grecaptcha.ready(function() {
                        grecaptcha.execute('6LemUeseAAAAADBntkIYpNjjo-yrBAeyR8utrb8Z', {action: action})
                            .then(function(token) {
                                if (token && token.length > 0) {
                                    resolve(token);
                                } else {
                                    reject(new Error('Empty token received'));
                                }
                            })
                            .catch(function(error) {
                                console.error('ReCAPTCHA execution error:', error);
                                reject(error);
                            });
                    });
                });
            };
        </script>
                
    <!-- Script pour exécuter reCAPTCHA avant soumission -->
    <script>
        (function() {
            const action = 'newsletter';
            const recaptchaFieldId = 'g-recaptcha-response-newsletter';
            
            function initializeRecaptcha() {
                const recaptchaField = document.getElementById(recaptchaFieldId);
                if (!recaptchaField) {
                    console.warn('Champ reCAPTCHA non trouvé:', recaptchaFieldId);
                    return;
                }
                
                const form = recaptchaField.closest('form');
                if (!form) {
                    console.warn('Formulaire non trouvé pour reCAPTCHA action:', action);
                    return;
                }
                
                // Éviter les doublons d'écouteurs d'événements
                if (form.hasAttribute('data-recaptcha-initialized-' + action)) {
                    return;
                }
                form.setAttribute('data-recaptcha-initialized-' + action, 'true');
                
                form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    
                    // Vérifier si reCAPTCHA est chargé
                    if (typeof window.executeRecaptcha !== 'function') {
                        console.error('Fonction executeRecaptcha non disponible');
                        alert('Erreur de configuration reCAPTCHA. Veuillez réessayer.');
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Exécuter reCAPTCHA
                    window.executeRecaptcha(action)
                        .then(function(token) {
                            if (token && token.length > 0) {
                                recaptchaField.value = token;
                                form.submit();
                            } else {
                                throw new Error('Token reCAPTCHA vide');
                            }
                        })
                        .catch(function(error) {
                            console.error('Erreur reCAPTCHA:', error);
                            alert('Erreur de vérification reCAPTCHA. Veuillez réessayer.');
                        });
                });
            }
            
            // Initialiser quand le DOM est prêt
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeRecaptcha);
            } else {
                initializeRecaptcha();
            }
        })();
    </script>
                     
                    <button type="submit"
                        class="w-full bg-samabac-600 hover:bg-samabac-700 text-white font-medium py-2 px-4 rounded-md transition-colors duration-200 flex items-center justify-center space-x-2">
                        <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"
                                d="M12 19l9 2-9-18-9 18 9-2zm0 0v-8"></path>
                        </svg>
                        <span>S'abonner</span>
                    </button>
                </form>

                <p class="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 mt-4 text-center">

    <!-- Bouton scroll to top (flottant en bas à droite) -->
    <button id="scroll-to-top"
        class="fixed bottom-6 right-6 w-12 h-12 bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg transition-colors z-50 opacity-0 pointer-events-none">
        <svg class="w-6 h-6 text-white" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M5 10l7-7m0 0l7 7m-7-7v18">
            </path>
        </svg>
    </button>
</footer>

<script>
    // Script pour le bouton scroll to top
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const scrollToTopBtn = document.getElementById('scroll-to-top');

        // Afficher/masquer le bouton selon la position de scroll
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            if (window.pageYOffset > 300) {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('opacity-100');
            } else {
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.add('opacity-0', 'pointer-events-none');
                scrollToTopBtn.classList.remove('opacity-100');
            }
        });

        // Scroll vers le haut au clic
        scrollToTopBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({
                top: 0,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        });

        // === GESTION MODAL NEWSLETTER ===
        const newsletterCta = document.getElementById('newsletter-cta');
        const newsletterModal = document.getElementById('newsletter-modal');
        const closeNewsletterModal = document.getElementById('close-newsletter-modal');
        const newsletterForm = document.getElementById('newsletter-form');

        // Ouvrir le modal
        newsletterCta.addEventListener('click', function() {
            newsletterModal.classList.remove('hidden');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; // Empêcher le scroll

            // Animation d'entrée
            setTimeout(() => {
                const modalContent = document.getElementById('newsletter-modal-content');
                modalContent.classList.remove('scale-95', 'opacity-0');
                modalContent.classList.add('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
            }, 10);
        });

        // Fermer le modal
        function closeModal() {
            const modalContent = document.getElementById('newsletter-modal-content');
            modalContent.classList.remove('scale-100', 'opacity-100');
            modalContent.classList.add('scale-95', 'opacity-0');

            setTimeout(() => {
                newsletterModal.classList.add('hidden');
                document.body.style.overflow = ''; // Restaurer le scroll
            }, 200);
        }

        closeNewsletterModal.addEventListener('click', closeModal);

        // Fermer en cliquant sur l'arrière-plan
        newsletterModal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (e.target === newsletterModal) {
                closeModal();
            }
        });

        // Fermer avec la touche Escape
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape' && !newsletterModal.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                closeModal();
            }
        });

        // Gestion de la soumission du formulaire
        newsletterForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const submitBtn = newsletterForm.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
            const originalText = submitBtn.innerHTML;

            // Désactiver le bouton et afficher un loader
            submitBtn.disabled = true;
            submitBtn.innerHTML = `
                <svg class="animate-spin w-4 h-4" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle>
                    <path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path>
                </svg>
                <span>Inscription...</span>
            `;

            // Récupérer les données du formulaire
            const formData = new FormData(newsletterForm);

            // Envoyer la requête
            fetch(newsletterForm.action, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData,
                    headers: {
                        'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest'
                    }
                })
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    if (data.success) {
                        // Succès - rediriger vers la page de confirmation
                        window.location.href = data.redirect_url;
                    } else {
                        // Erreur - afficher les messages d'erreur
                        showFormErrors(data.errors);
                        submitBtn.disabled = false;
                        submitBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
                    }
                })
                .catch(error => {
                    console.error('Erreur:', error);
                    // En cas d'erreur, soumettre le formulaire normalement
                    newsletterForm.submit();
                });
        });

        // Fonction pour afficher les erreurs de validation
        function showFormErrors(errors) {
            // Supprimer les anciens messages d'erreur
            newsletterForm.querySelectorAll('.error-message').forEach(el => el.remove());
            newsletterForm.querySelectorAll('.border-red-500').forEach(el => {
                el.classList.remove('border-red-500');
                el.classList.add('border-gray-300', 'dark:border-gray-600');
            });

            // Afficher les nouveaux messages d'erreur
            Object.keys(errors).forEach(field => {
                const input = newsletterForm.querySelector(`[name="${field}"]`);
                if (input) {
                    input.classList.remove('border-gray-300', 'dark:border-gray-600');
                    input.classList.add('border-red-500');

                    const errorDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    errorDiv.className = 'error-message text-red-600 text-sm mt-1';
                    errorDiv.textContent = errors[field][0];
                    input.parentNode.appendChild(errorDiv);
                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>

    <!-- Body End Scripts -->
    
    <!-- Custom JavaScript -->
    
    <!-- Page Scripts -->
        <script>
        (function() {
            const adElement = document.querySelector('[data-ad-id="3"]');
            if (!adElement) return;

            const adId = 3;
            let impressionRecorded = false;

            // Fonction pour enregistrer une impression
            function recordImpression() {
                if (impressionRecorded) return;
                
                // Vérifier si l'élément est visible dans le viewport
                const rect = adElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                const isVisible = rect.top < window.innerHeight && rect.bottom > 0;
                
                if (!isVisible) return;

                impressionRecorded = true;

                // Enregistrer l'impression via AJAX
                fetch('https://samabac.sn/advertisements/3/impression', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'X-CSRF-TOKEN': 'Svh2djVHVvs6LXtHpp8YStShzNu32lUHtguw1taK'
                    },
                    credentials: 'same-origin'
                }).catch(err => console.error('Erreur enregistrement impression:', err));
            }

            // Observer pour détecter quand la pub entre dans le viewport
            if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
                const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
                    entries.forEach(entry => {
                        if (entry.isIntersecting && !impressionRecorded) {
                            // Délai de 1 seconde pour confirmer que l'utilisateur voit vraiment la pub
                            setTimeout(recordImpression, 1000);
                        }
                    });
                }, {
                    threshold: 0.5 // Au moins 50% de la pub visible
                });

                observer.observe(adElement);
            } else {
                // Fallback pour les navigateurs sans IntersectionObserver
                window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
                    if (!impressionRecorded) {
                        recordImpression();
                    }
                }, { once: true });
            }

            // Gérer les clics sur les bannières (déjà géré par le lien dans getBannerHtml)
        })();
    </script>
